    massCode 3.0 â€” A free and open source code snippet manager for developers
    What it is and why massCode is a snippet manager for developers that helps you conveniently organize pieces of code and have quick access to them. Multilevel folders and tags are used for organization, and each snippet has fragments for even more granular structuring. The app supports Markdown so it can be used as a notebook if needed. What's New Direct support for TextMate grammars Now massCode uses Codemirror as the basis for the editor and `.tmLanguage` as the grammar for syntax highlighting. This tandem opens the door to over 600 existing grammars. The application currently supports more than 160 grammars. In addition to `.tmLanguage`, the application supports `.tmTheme` for themes. Real-time Render for HTML & CSS Now you can see the result of HTML & CSS directly in the application. This is such a CodePen on minimal :) Mermaid Diagram Added support for Mermaid - diagramming and charting tool that renders Markdown-inspired text definitions to create and modify diagrams dynamically. Presentation Mode massCode allows you to make a presentation out of a sequence of snippets. It's great for classroom use, team meetings, conferences or simply reviewing notes on your own. Screnshots Create beautiful snippet images on different backgrounds and in different modes. Sometimes these pet ideas do not make it through the product management feature-selection process. Other times, a developer does not have time to complete the solution end-to-end on their own, yet they know if it could somehow be implemented, the project would benefit.     UpSavvy â€” Helping K-12 school districts solve digital citizenship
    Why is digital citizenship important to teach? Some stats from the USA: - 93% of young people aged 8-18 owned a smartphone in 2021 - 37% of young people between the ages of 12 and 17 have been cyberbullied - Teens who spend 5 or more hours online a day are 71% more likely than those who spend only 1 hour a day to have at least one suicide risk factor - 89% of sexual advances directed at young people occur through instant messaging & chatroom - 80% of middle schoolers believed that an advertisement labeled as sponsored content was actually a news story - 60% of educational organizations experienced phishing attacks in 2020 - Ransomware attacks on US schools and colleges cost $3.5 billion in 2021 Through research and discussions with K-12 school districts, we learned that digital citizenship is a priority, but districts lack the tools to deliver up-to-date content at scale and measure results. Teachers also have very limited amounts of time to effectively incorporate digital citizenship lessons into their curriculum. We also learned that students are becoming accustomed to learning through short form video content. Why UpSavvy works: - Takes students less than 5 minutes a month to learn digital citizenship. - Interactive content with over 200 bite size videos, quizzes & simulations. - Empowers teachers with resources while minimizing their time investment. - Enhances the classroom experience without sacrificing learning time. - Integrates directly with school district rostering & LMS systems including Clever, Classlink, Google & Microsoft - Curriculum covers topics: Privacy & Security, Digital Well-Being, Cyberbullying, Digital Footprint, Media Literacy, Technology Essentials, Online Relationships & Safety, Digital Commerce, Digital Finance As parents and technology experts, our mission is to help K-12 students make better decisions online.
